  <script>
    function countdownRedirect(countdownSeconds, redirectUrl) {
      var countdown = countdownSeconds;

      function updateCountdown() {
        document.getElementById('countdown').textContent = countdown;
        countdown--;

        if (countdown < 0) {
            window.location.href = redirectUrl;
        } else {
            setTimeout(updateCountdown, 1000);
        }
      }

      updateCountdown();
    }
  </script>
  <h1>404 - 该页面没找到</h1>
  <p>该页面将在<span id="countdown"></span>秒后返回首页</p>
  <script>
    // 调用倒计时函数，传入参数：倒计时秒数和重定向页面的URL
    countdownRedirect(5, '/');
</script>

              </article>

  <script>
    var marquee = document.getElementById('marquee');
    var isPaused = false;

    function stopMarquee() {
      if (!isPaused) {
        marquee.stop();
        isPaused = true;
      }
    }

    function startMarquee() {
      if (isPaused) {
        marquee.start();
        isPaused = false;
      }
    }
  </script>
